Hey Eystreem! I love your mythbusters series, and i have an idea for the next video. One time, i was playing minecraft with my friend, and everything was normal. Keep in mind, (This will be important for you to bust this) We were in the first ever released version of Minecraft Preview. Anyways, i was making a Hotspring, and my friend was checking out the new update. In the middle of me building, He asked for me to check something out. Since im a Mythbuster fan, he called me over to explain some special blocks he found. It was an Update block. I said "Dont worry, those are just unloaded blocks. He went on with his business, and so did i. Later, i was building and again, something happened. However, way more worrying. I went in chat and i saw a message from a player who went by the name of " Unknown". He spoke in an Unidentified language. I got confused. Then, my friend typed in all caps, "HUH?!" He told me to follow him into the nether. Two words. World. GEN. There was a water pool?! Whats weirder, It was BLOOD WATER. I was pretty sure it was a render glitch, but i was very skeptical too. Soon after, i went back to the overworld and i was put in survival mode by the entity, and i could not change back. The entity said nothing. We were very unsettled, but we brushed it off and made a new World. You can guess what happened. The entity stayed quiet a bit, so we made a house, and went to a cave to mine. But then, it said "Killcode injected." We jumped. We ignored it to see what would happen, and we went mining again. But then, we found a command block. I went into creative to check it out, and it said the text command for the message we saw earlier. I closed it and looked again, IT WAS GONE. For a long time, it never messed with us again, but if you use this comment for a video, i will tell you guys the part 2!
